# Introduction | Hyperliquid

A community-supported [Hyperliquid APIarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api)
 SDK for all major JS runtimes, written in TypeScript.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#installation)

Installation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

npm

pnpm

yarn

bun

deno

CDN

Copy

    npm i @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    pnpm add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    yarn add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    bun add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    deno add jsr:@nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    <script type="module">
      import * as hl from "https://esm.sh/jsr/@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    </script>

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#quick-start)

Quick start


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

InfoClient

ExchangeClient

SubscriptionClient

Read market data, account state, order book. [Learn more](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#read-data)

Copy

    import { HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    const mids = await client.allMids();

Place orders, transfer funds, manage accounts. [Learn more](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#trading)

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });
    
    await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: 0,\
        b: true,\
        p: "50000",\
        s: "0.01",\
        r: false,\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

Receive real-time updates via WebSocket. [Learn more](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#real-time-updates)

Copy

    import { SubscriptionClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    const client = new SubscriptionClient({ transport });
    
    await client.allMids((data) => {
      console.log(data.mids);
    });

[NextConnect to Hyperliquidchevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports)

# Connect to Hyperliquid | Hyperliquid

The SDK communicates with Hyperliquid through a transport. Choose HTTP or WebSocket and pass it to any [client](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients)
.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#http-vs-websocket)

HTTP vs WebSocket


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following table compares the two transport types:

HTTP

WebSocket

**Best for**

Serverless, simple scripts

Real-time data, low latency

**Connection**

Per-request, stateless

Persistent

**Subscriptions**

No

Required

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#http)

HTTP


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    import { HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    const mids = await client.allMids();

Each request is an independent HTTP POST. No connection state to manage, so it works well in serverless functions, edge workers, or unstable networks.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#endpoints)

Endpoints

Two built-in endpoints: `apiUrl` for info and exchange requests, `rpcUrl` for explorer requests (block details, transactions). The following table lists the default URLs:

Mainnet

Testnet

`apiUrl`

`https://api.hyperliquid.xyz`

`https://api.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz`

`rpcUrl`

`https://rpc.hyperliquid.xyz`

`https://rpc.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz`

Override when running your [own nodearrow-up-right](https://github.com/hyperliquid-dex/node)
 or using a proxy:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#fetch-options)

Fetch options

Pass custom options to the underlying [`fetch`arrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Fetch_API)
 call, such as headers, credentials, and cache settings.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#websocket)

WebSocket


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The transport maintains a single persistent connection, required for [subscriptionsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/websocket/subscriptions)
 and lower-latency for high-frequency [POST requestsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/websocket/post-requests)
:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#endpoints-1)

Endpoints

`url` for info, exchange, and subscription requests. Explorer requests (block details, transactions) need a separate transport on the RPC endpoint. The following table lists the default URLs:

Mainnet

Testnet

`url`

`wss://api.hyperliquid.xyz/ws`

`wss://api.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz/ws`

`MAINNET_RPC_WS_URL`

`wss://rpc.hyperliquid.xyz/ws`

`TESTNET_RPC_WS_URL`

`wss://rpc.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz/ws`

Override when running your [own nodearrow-up-right](https://github.com/hyperliquid-dex/node)
 or using a proxy:

For explorer, pass the RPC constant as `url`:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#reconnection)

Reconnection

When the connection drops, the transport reconnects automatically via [`@nktkas/rews`arrow-up-right](https://github.com/nktkas/rews)
:

See [`ReconnectingWebSocketOptions`arrow-up-right](https://github.com/nktkas/rews#options)
 for all available options.

* * *

After reconnection, all active subscriptions are restored automatically. Disable this with `resubscribe`:

If a subscription fails to restore, its `failureSignal` is aborted. For details, see [Handle failures](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#handle-failures)
.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#common-options)

Common options


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#testnet)

Testnet

Connect to the Hyperliquid testnet for development and testing:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#timeout)

Timeout

Both transports abort requests after 10 seconds by default. Set a custom timeout or `null` to disable:

[PreviousIntroductionchevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid)
[NextClientschevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients)

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport({
      apiUrl: "https://custom-api.example.com",
      rpcUrl: "https://custom-rpc.example.com",
    });

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport({
      fetchOptions: {
        headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer ..." },
      },
    });

Copy

    import { SubscriptionClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    const client = new SubscriptionClient({ transport });
    
    await client.allMids((data) => {
      console.log(data.mids);
    });

Copy

    import { InfoClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    const mids = await client.allMids();

Copy

    import { WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({
      url: "wss://custom-api.example.com/ws",
    });

Copy

    import { MAINNET_RPC_WS_URL, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const explorerTransport = new WebSocketTransport({ url: MAINNET_RPC_WS_URL });

Copy

    import { WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({
      reconnect: {
        maxRetries: 10,
        reconnectionDelay: 1_000,
      },
    });

Copy

    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({ resubscribe: false });

Copy

    const transport = new HttpTransport({ isTestnet: true });
    // or
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({ isTestnet: true });

Copy

    const transport = new HttpTransport({ timeout: 30_000 });
    // or
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({ timeout: 30_000 });

# Market orders | Hyperliquid

Hyperliquid doesn't have a dedicated market order type. Simulate market orders using a limit order with `tif: "Ioc"` (Immediate or Cancel) and a price that guarantees immediate execution.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/market-orders#ioc-order-workflow)

IoC order workflow


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An IoC order fills immediately at the best available price and cancels any unfilled portion. Set the price aggressively to ensure a fill:

*   **Buy:** price above current mid (for example, +1%)
    
*   **Sell:** price below current mid (for example, -1%)
    

The 1% buffer is a starting point. Volatile markets or large orders may need a wider margin.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/market-orders#example)

Example


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { formatPrice, formatSize, SymbolConverter } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({ transport });
    const info = new InfoClient({ transport });
    const exchange = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });
    
    // Parameters
    const coin = "ETH";
    const size = "0.1";
    const isBuy = true;
    const tolerance = 0.01; // 1% price buffer
    
    // Get aggressive price based on current mid price with tolerance
    const mids = await info.allMids();
    const mid = parseFloat(mids[coin]);
    const price = mid * (1 + (isBuy ? tolerance : -tolerance));
    
    // ! asserts the symbol exists - handle undefined in production
    const assetId = converter.getAssetId(coin)!;
    const szDecimals = converter.getSzDecimals(coin)!;
    
    // Place IoC order with aggressive price to ensure fill
    await exchange.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: assetId,\
        b: isBuy,\
        p: formatPrice(price, szDecimals),\
        s: formatSize(size, szDecimals),\
        r: false,\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Ioc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

[PreviousSigningchevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing)
[NextAgent wallets and vaultschevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults)

# Utilities | Hyperliquid

Helper functions for formatting orders and resolving asset symbols, imported from `@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils`.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#format-prices)

Format prices


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`formatPrice` truncates a price to the Hyperliquid [tick sizearrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/tick-and-lot-size)
 precision.

Copy

    import { formatPrice } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    
    formatPrice("97123.456789", 0); // "97123"
    formatPrice("1.23456789", 5); // "1.2"
    formatPrice("0.0000123456789", 0, "spot"); // "0.00001234"

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#format-sizes)

Format sizes


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`formatSize` truncates a size to the asset [lot sizearrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/tick-and-lot-size)
 precision.

Copy

    import { formatSize } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    
    formatSize("1.23456789", 5); // "1.23456"
    formatSize("0.123456789", 2); // "0.12"
    formatSize("100", 0); // "100"

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#resolve-symbols)

Resolve symbols


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`SymbolConverter` maps human-readable symbols to Hyperliquid [asset IDsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/asset-ids)
 and formatting metadata. It fetches data from the API on creation.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#asset-ids)

Asset IDs

`getAssetId` returns the numeric ID used in order parameters:

Perpetuals use the coin name. Spot markets use `"BASE/QUOTE"` format. Returns `undefined` if the symbol is not found.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#size-decimals)

Size decimals

`getSzDecimals` returns the lot size precision for an asset:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#spot-pair-ids)

Spot pair IDs

`getSpotPairId` returns the identifier used in info requests and subscriptions for spot markets:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#refresh-data)

Refresh data

Call `reload` to update the symbol mappings when new assets are listed:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#builder-dex-support)

Builder DEX support

Pass `dexs` to include assets from [builder DEXsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/hyperliquid-improvement-proposals-hips/hip-3-builder-deployed-perpetuals)
:

Builder DEX assets use `"DEX:ASSET"` format:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#format-and-place-an-order)

Format and place an order


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[PreviousError handlingchevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling)

*   [Asset IDs](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#asset-ids)
    
*   [Size decimals](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#size-decimals)
    
*   [Spot pair IDs](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#spot-pair-ids)
    
*   [Refresh data](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#refresh-data)
    
*   [Builder DEX support](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#builder-dex-support)
    
*   [Format and place an order](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities#format-and-place-an-order)

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { SymbolConverter } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({ transport });

Copy

    converter.getAssetId("BTC"); // 0
    converter.getAssetId("HYPE/USDC"); // 10107

Copy

    converter.getSzDecimals("BTC"); // 5
    converter.getSzDecimals("HYPE/USDC"); // 2

Copy

    converter.getSpotPairId("HYPE/USDC"); // "@107"
    converter.getSpotPairId("PURR/USDC"); // "PURR/USDC"

Copy

    await converter.reload();

Copy

    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({
      transport,
      dexs: true, // all DEXs
    });

Copy

    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({
      transport,
      dexs: ["test", "other"], // specific DEXs
    });

Copy

    converter.getAssetId("test:ABC"); // 110000
    converter.getSzDecimals("test:ABC"); // 0

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { formatPrice, formatSize, SymbolConverter } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({ transport });
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });
    
    // Parameters
    const coin = "BTC";
    const price = "97123.456789";
    const size = "0.00123456789";
    const isBuy = true;
    
    // ! asserts the symbol exists - handle undefined in production
    const assetId = converter.getAssetId(coin)!;
    const szDecimals = converter.getSzDecimals(coin)!;
    
    await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: assetId, // asset index\
        b: isBuy, // buy\
        p: formatPrice(price, szDecimals), // price\
        s: formatSize(size, szDecimals), // size\
        r: false, // not reduce-only\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } }, // Good-Til-Cancelled\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

# Error handling | Hyperliquid

The SDK throws `HyperliquidError` and its subclasses. Each subclass represents a specific failure category, such as validation, transport, API, or wallet errors.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#error-hierarchy)

Error hierarchy


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    Error
    └─ HyperliquidError
       ├─ ValidationError
       ├─ AbstractWalletError
       ├─ TransportError
       │  ├─ HttpRequestError
       │  └─ WebSocketRequestError
       └─ ApiRequestError

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#transport-errors)

Transport errors


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These errors are thrown when the request itself fails, such as network issues, timeouts, or non-JSON responses.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#httprequesterror)

HttpRequestError

This error is thrown when an HTTP request fails, such as non-200 status codes, non-JSON responses, or network-level failures.

Has `response` (the [`Response`arrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Response)
 object) when the server responded, `undefined` for network-level failures.

Copy

    import { HttpRequestError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.allMids();
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof HttpRequestError) {
        console.error(error.message); // "429 Too Many Requests - ..."
        console.error(error.response?.status); // 429
        console.error(await error.response?.text()); // response body
      }
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#websocketrequesterror)

WebSocketRequestError

This error is thrown when a WebSocket request or subscription fails, such as connection failures, server errors, or exceeded subscription limits.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#api-errors)

API errors


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`ApiRequestError` is thrown when the Hyperliquid API processes the request but returns an error, such as insufficient margin, invalid price, or unknown wallet address.

Has `response` with the full API response object:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#wallet-errors)

Wallet errors


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`AbstractWalletError` is thrown when a wallet operation fails, such as signature creation, address retrieval, or chain ID detection. The original error is in `cause`.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#validation-errors)

Validation errors


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`ValidationError` is thrown when request parameters fail schema validation before sending.

The `cause` property contains the original [`ValiError`arrow-up-right](https://valibot.dev/api/ValiError/)
 with detailed issue information:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#timeouts-and-cancellation)

Timeouts and cancellation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Both transports use [`AbortSignal`arrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/AbortSignal)
 internally, so timeouts and user-initiated cancellations produce a [`DOMException`arrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/DOMException)
 in `cause`:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#catch-all-errors)

Catch all errors


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[PreviousClientschevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients)
[NextUtilitieschevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities)

Last updated 4 days ago

*   [Error hierarchy](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#error-hierarchy)
    
*   [Transport errors](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#transport-errors)
    
*   [HttpRequestError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#httprequesterror)
    
*   [WebSocketRequestError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#websocketrequesterror)
    
*   [API errors](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#api-errors)
    
*   [Wallet errors](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#wallet-errors)
    
*   [Validation errors](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#validation-errors)
    
*   [Timeouts and cancellation](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#timeouts-and-cancellation)
    
*   [Catch all errors](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/error-handling#catch-all-errors)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    import { WebSocketRequestError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.allMids();
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof WebSocketRequestError) {
        console.error(error.message); // for example, "WebSocket connection closed"
      }
    }

Copy

    import { ApiRequestError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.order({ orders: [/* ... */], grouping: "na" });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof ApiRequestError) {
        console.error(error.message); // for example, "Insufficient margin to place order"
        console.error(error.response); // full API response
      }
    }

Copy

    import { AbstractWalletError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.order({ orders: [/* ... */], grouping: "na" });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof AbstractWalletError) {
        console.error(error.message); // for example, "Failed to sign typed data with viem wallet"
        console.error(error.cause); // original wallet error
      }
    }

Copy

    import { ValidationError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.order({ orders: [/* ... */], grouping: "na" });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof ValidationError) {
        console.error(error.message); // human-readable validation message
        console.error(error.cause.issues); // detailed list of validation issues
      }
    }

Copy

    import { TransportError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    //       ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
    //       universal transport error superclass for both HTTP and WebSocket transports
    
    try {
      await client.allMids();
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof TransportError && error.cause instanceof DOMException) {
        if (error.cause.name === "TimeoutError") {
          // Transport timeout (default 10 s)
        }
        if (error.cause.name === "AbortError") {
          // Cancelled via AbortSignal
        }
      }
    }

Copy

    import {
      AbstractWalletError,
      ApiRequestError,
      HttpRequestError,
      HyperliquidError,
      TransportError,
      ValidationError,
      WebSocketRequestError,
    } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.order({ orders: [/* ... */], grouping: "na" });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof HyperliquidError) {
        if (error instanceof ValidationError) {
          // Invalid parameters - check error.message, error.cause
        } else if (error instanceof ApiRequestError) {
          // API rejected the action - check error.message
        } else if (error instanceof AbstractWalletError) {
          // Wallet failed - check error.cause
        } else if (error instanceof TransportError) {
          if (error instanceof HttpRequestError) {
            // HTTP failure - check error.response, error.cause
          } else if (error instanceof WebSocketRequestError) {
            // WebSocket failure - check error.message
          }
        } else {
          // Unexpected HyperliquidError subclass - check error.message
        }
      }
      throw error; // re-throw unexpected errors
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Agent wallets and vaults | Hyperliquid

Hyperliquid supports delegated trading through [agent walletsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets#api-wallets)
, and isolated capital through [vaults and sub-accountsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#subaccounts-and-vaults)
.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#agent-wallets)

Agent wallets


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An agent wallet signs trades on behalf of your master account. Approve it once, then use the agent's private key for all subsequent requests:

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."), // agent's private key
    });
    
    // All trades are executed as the master account
    await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: 0,\
        b: true,\
        p: "50000",\
        s: "0.01",\
        r: false,\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#create-an-agent)

Create an agent

Approve an agent via `approveAgent` or through the [Hyperliquid UIarrow-up-right](https://app.hyperliquid.xyz/API)
:

Agents expire after 90 days by default. To set a custom expiration (up to 180 days), append `valid_until <timestamp>` to the name:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#vaults)

Vaults


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A vault is an isolated trading account that other users can deposit into. Trade on behalf of a vault by setting `vaultAddress`:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#manage-vaults)

Manage vaults

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#sub-accounts)

Sub-accounts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sub-accounts work like vaults but belong to a single user. They share the same `vaultAddress` mechanism for trading:

[PreviousMarket orderschevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/market-orders)
[NextBrowser walletschevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/browser-wallets)

Last updated 5 days ago

*   [Agent wallets](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#agent-wallets)
    
*   [Create an agent](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#create-an-agent)
    
*   [Vaults](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#vaults)
    
*   [Manage vaults](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#manage-vaults)
    
*   [Sub-accounts](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#sub-accounts)

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."), // master account
    });
    
    await client.approveAgent({
      agentAddress: "0x...", // address of the agent wallet
      agentName: "my-bot",
    });

Copy

    const timestamp = Date.now() + 180 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 180 days from now
    await client.approveAgent({
      agentAddress: "0x...",
      agentName: `my-bot valid_until ${timestamp}`,
    });

Copy

    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet,
      defaultVaultAddress: "0x...",
    });

Copy

    await client.order({ orders: [/* ... */], grouping: "na" }, {
      vaultAddress: "0x...",
    });

Copy

    // Create
    const result = await client.createVault({
      name: "My Vault",
      description: "Automated trading strategy",
      initialUsd: 100e6, // 100 USD in microunits
      nonce: Date.now(),
    });
    
    // Deposit
    await client.vaultTransfer({
      vaultAddress: "0x...",
      isDeposit: true,
      usd: 50e6, // 50 USD in microunits
    });
    
    // Withdraw
    await client.vaultTransfer({
      vaultAddress: "0x...",
      isDeposit: false,
      usd: 25e6, // 25 USD in microunits
    });

Copy

    // Create
    const result = await client.createSubAccount({ name: "trading-bot" });
    const subAccountAddress = result.response.data;
    
    // Transfer funds
    await client.subAccountTransfer({
      subAccountUser: subAccountAddress,
      isDeposit: true,
      usd: 10e6, // 10 USD in microunits
    });
    
    // Transfer spot tokens
    await client.subAccountSpotTransfer({
      subAccountUser: subAccountAddress,
      isDeposit: true,
      token: "USDC:0xeb62eee3685fc4c43992febcd9e75443",
      amount: "100", // 100 USDC
    });
    
    // Trade on behalf of sub-account
    await client.order({ orders: [/* ... */], grouping: "na" }, {
      vaultAddress: subAccountAddress,
    });

# Tree-shaking | Hyperliquid

The SDK is organized into modular entry points so bundlers can eliminate unused code.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/tree-shaking#entry-points)

Entry points


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following table lists the available entry points:

Entry point

Contains

`@nktkas/hyperliquid`

Transports, clients, error classes

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing`

Signing functions, wallet utilities

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils`

`formatPrice`, `formatSize`, `SymbolConverter`

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/info`

Info methods, individually importable

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange`

Exchange methods, individually importable

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/subscription`

Subscription methods, individually importable

Each entry point has independent dependencies. Importing `@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils` doesn't pull in signing or validation code.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/tree-shaking#direct-method-imports)

Direct method imports


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Instead of creating a [client](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients)
 (which bundles all methods), import individual methods directly. Each method accepts the same config as its client as the first argument.

Info methods use [`InfoClient`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#read-data)
 config:

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { allMids } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/info";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const result = await allMids({ transport });

This bundles only the `allMids` method, its validation schema, and the transport logic — not the full `InfoClient` with all methods.

Exchange methods use [`ExchangeClient`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#trading)
 config:

Subscription methods use [`SubscriptionClient`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#real-time-updates)
 config:

[PreviousBrowser walletschevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/browser-wallets)
[NextInfo Methodschevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/api-reference/info-methods)

Last updated 5 days ago

*   [Entry points](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/tree-shaking#entry-points)
    
*   [Direct method imports](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/tree-shaking#direct-method-imports)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { order } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    await order(
      { transport, wallet },
      {
        orders: [{\
          a: 0,\
          b: true,\
          p: "50000",\
          s: "0.01",\
          r: false,\
          t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
        }],
        grouping: "na",
      },
    );

Copy

    import { WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { allMids } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/subscription";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    const subscription = await allMids({ transport }, (data) => {
      console.log(data.mids);
    });

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Clients | Hyperliquid

A client uses a [transport](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports)
 to call a specific part of the Hyperliquid API:

*   **Info:** market data, account state, blockchain explorer
    
*   **Exchange:** trading, fund management, account configuration
    
*   **Subscription:** real-time updates via WebSocket
    

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#read-data)

Read data


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`InfoClient` gives read-only access to the [Info endpointarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/info-endpoint)
. Works with any transport.

Copy

    import { HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    const mids = await client.allMids();
    const book = await client.l2Book({ coin: "ETH" });

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#trading)

Trading


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

`ExchangeClient` executes actions on the [Exchange endpointarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint)
: trading, fund management, and account configuration. Requires a wallet for [signing](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#wallet-compatibility)
 and works with any transport.

viem

ethers

Browser (viem)

Browser (ethers)

Custom

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."),
    });

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { Wallet } from "ethers";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet: new Wallet("0x..."),
    });

Use a [JSON-RPC Accountarrow-up-right](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)
 to connect browser extensions like MetaMask:

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { createWalletClient, custom } from "viem";
    import { arbitrum } from "viem/chains";
    
    const wallet = createWalletClient({
      chain: arbitrum,
      transport: custom(window.ethereum!),
    });
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });

Use a [BrowserProviderarrow-up-right](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/providers/#BrowserProvider)
 to connect browser extensions like MetaMask:

Any object matching one of the [supported wallet interfaces](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#wallet-compatibility)
 works. The minimum requirement is [`signTypedData`arrow-up-right](https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-712)
 and an address:

Place an order:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#multi-sig)

Multi-sig

[Multi-signature accountsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/hypercore/multi-sig)
 require multiple authorized signers to approve every action. The **leader** (first signer in the array) collects all signatures and submits the final transaction — only the leader's nonce is validated by the server.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#vault-and-sub-account-trading)

Vault and sub-account trading

To trade on behalf of a [vault or sub-accountarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#subaccounts-and-vaults)
, set a default or pass `vaultAddress` per-request:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#expiration)

Expiration

A server-side guard. The API rejects the action after this timestamp (milliseconds). See [Expires Afterarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#expires-after)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#signature-chain-id)

Signature chain ID

Sets the EIP-712 domain `chainId` for [user-signed actions](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#user-signed-action-protocol)
. Defaults to the wallet's provider chain ID. Local wallets without a provider (e.g., [`privateKeyToAccount`arrow-up-right](https://viem.sh/docs/accounts/local/privateKeyToAccount)
, [`new Wallet()`arrow-up-right](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/wallet/#Wallet)
) fall back to `0x1` (Ethereum mainnet). Override to set the correct chain:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#nonce-manager)

Nonce manager

The SDK generates [noncesarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets#hyperliquid-nonces)
 automatically using timestamps with auto-increment. Replace it if you need custom logic:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#real-time-updates)

Real-time updates


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`SubscriptionClient` streams live data via [WebSocket subscriptionsarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/websocket/subscriptions)
. Requires [`WebSocketTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#websocket)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#unsubscribe)

Unsubscribe

A single connection supports up to [1000 active subscriptions and 10 unique usersarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/rate-limits-and-user-limits)
. Call `unsubscribe()` to remove a listener and free these slots:

Subscribing to the same channel multiple times reuses one underlying subscription. Each `unsubscribe()` removes only its listener — the channel stays open until the last one is removed:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#handle-failures)

Handle failures

When the WebSocket [reconnects](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports#reconnection)
, the SDK automatically resubscribes to all active channels. If resubscription fails for a channel, its `failureSignal` aborts with the error:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#common-options)

Common options


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#cancellation)

Cancellation

`InfoClient` methods accept an optional [`AbortSignal`arrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/AbortSignal)
 as the last argument:

`ExchangeClient` methods accept it inside the options object (also last argument). Unlike [Expiration](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#expiration)
, which is a server-side guard, cancellation aborts the request on the client side before or during delivery:

[PreviousConnect to Hyperliquidchevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/transports)

---

# Signing | Hyperliquid

Every exchange action on Hyperliquid requires an [EIP-712arrow-up-right](https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-712)
 signature. [`ExchangeClient`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/clients#trading)
 handles this automatically. The following functions are for custom integrations or actions not yet supported by `ExchangeClient`.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#how-signing-works)

How signing works


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hyperliquid has two signing flows depending on the action type:

L1 actions

User-signed actions

**Examples**

Trading and position management

Fund movements and account security

**EIP-712 domain**

`Exchange`, chain ID `1337`

`HyperliquidSignTransaction`, user's chain ID

**What gets signed**

Action hash as `connectionId`

Action fields directly

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#l1-action)

L1 action

The action is never signed directly. Instead, a **phantom agent** is constructed:

1.  [Msgpackarrow-up-right](https://msgpack.org/)
    \-encode the action object (field order matters — the expected order varies by action type)
    
2.  Append the [noncearrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets)
     as uint64 big-endian (8 bytes)
    
3.  Append a [vaultarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/hypercore/vaults)
     marker: `0x01` + 20-byte vault address, or `0x00` if none
    
4.  If [`expiresAfter`arrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#expires-after)
     is set, append `0x00` + the timestamp as uint64 big-endian
    
5.  [Keccak-256arrow-up-right](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SHA-3#Instances)
     hash the concatenated bytes. This is the `connectionId`
    
6.  Sign an [EIP-712arrow-up-right](https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-712)
     message with:
    
    *   Domain: `{ name: "Exchange", version: "1", chainId: 1337, verifyingContract: 0x0...0 }`
        
    *   Type: `Agent { source: string, connectionId: bytes32 }`
        
    *   Message: `{ source: "a" (mainnet) or "b" (testnet), connectionId }` where `connectionId` is the hash from step 5
        
    
7.  Send `{ action, signature: { r, s, v }, nonce }` to the [exchange endpointarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint)
    

Chain ID `1337` is hardcoded and doesn't depend on the wallet's network. The phantom agent construct means the validator recovers the signer from the `Agent` message, then verifies that the `connectionId` matches the action hash.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#user-signed-action)

User-signed action

The action fields are placed directly into the EIP-712 message, with no hashing or phantom agent:

1.  Each action type defines its own [typed dataarrow-up-right](https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-712#definition-of-typed-structured-data-%F0%9D%95%8A)
     structure (for example, `HyperliquidTransaction:ApproveAgent`)
    
2.  Sign an EIP-712 message with:
    
    *   Domain: `{ name: "HyperliquidSignTransaction", version: "1", chainId: <signatureChainId>, verifyingContract: 0x0...0 }`
        
    *   Type and message: defined per action
        
    
3.  Send `{ action, signature: { r, s, v }, nonce }` to the exchange endpoint
    

The `signatureChainId` field in the action (hex, such as `"0x66eee"`) sets the EIP-712 domain chain ID.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#common-rules)

Common rules

Both flows share:

*   **Nonce:** current timestamp in milliseconds. Hyperliquid stores the 100 highest nonces per signer and rejects duplicates. See [Noncesarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets)
    .
    
*   **Signature:** ECDSA `{ r, s, v }` where `v` is `27` or `28`
    
*   **Hex strings:** lowercase all hex values before signing
    

The following functions implement these flows. Each accepts any [compatible wallet](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#wallet-compatibility)
.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#l1-actions)

L1 actions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`signL1Action` signs an [L1 action](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#l1-action)
 and returns an ECDSA signature.

Use `isTestnet: true` when signing for the testnet — this changes the EIP-712 source from `"a"` to `"b"`.

viem

ethers

Browser (viem)

Browser (ethers)

Custom

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#user-signed-actions)

User-signed actions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`signUserSignedAction` signs a [user-signed action](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#user-signed-action)
 and returns an ECDSA signature.

Each action type has its own EIP-712 types, exported from `@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange` using the convention `PascalCase(actionType) + "Types"` (for example, `Withdraw3Types` for `withdraw3`, `ApproveAgentTypes` for `approveAgent`).

viem

ethers

Browser (viem)

Browser (ethers)

Custom

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#action-hashing)

Action hashing


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`createL1ActionHash` produces the keccak256 hash used as `connectionId` in L1 signing. Use it to verify that your action serialization matches what the SDK produces:

circle-exclamation

The hash depends on key order in the action object. The expected order varies by action type.

Optional parameters `vaultAddress` and `expiresAfter` are included in the hash when present.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#multi-sig-actions)

Multi-sig actions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`signMultiSigAction` signs the [multi-sigarrow-up-right](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/hypercore/multi-sig)
 wrapper after all signers have signed the inner action. The inner signing differs for L1 and user-signed actions. Use `isTestnet: true` when signing for the testnet, as with `signL1Action`.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#l1-actions-1)

L1 actions

Each signer signs the `[multiSigUser, outerSigner, action]` tuple via `signL1Action`. The leader (first signer) then signs the wrapper via `signMultiSigAction`:

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#user-signed)

User-signed

Each signer signs the action with embedded `payloadMultiSigUser` and `outerSigner` fields via `signUserSignedAction`. The leader then signs the wrapper via `signMultiSigAction`:

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#wallet-compatibility)

Wallet compatibility


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All signing functions accept `AbstractWallet` — a union of supported wallet interfaces:

`signTypedData`

Address

Chain ID

[viem Local Accountarrow-up-right](https://viem.sh/docs/accounts/local)

1 param (object)

`address` property

fallback `0x1`

[viem JSON-RPC Accountarrow-up-right](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)

1 param (object)

`getAddresses()`

`getChainId()`

[ethers Signerarrow-up-right](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/providers/#Signer)

3 params

`getAddress()`

`provider.getNetwork()`

Any object matching one of these interfaces works. See the [Custom tab](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#l1-actions)
 in signing examples.

### 

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#helpers)

Helpers

These functions work with any supported wallet type:

*   `getWalletAddress` — returns the wallet address, always lowercase
    
*   `getWalletChainId` — returns the wallet chain ID as hex, falls back to `"0x1"` for local wallets without a provider

[NextMarket orderschevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/market-orders)

    import { signL1Action } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const action = { type: "cancel", cancels: [{ a: 0, o: 12345 }] };
    const nonce = Date.now();
    
    const signature = await signL1Action({ wallet, action, nonce });
    
    await fetch("https://api.hyperliquid.xyz/exchange", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ action, signature, nonce }),
    });

    import { ApproveAgentTypes } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";

      type: "approveAgent",
      signatureChainId: "0x66eee",
      hyperliquidChain: "Mainnet",
      agentAddress: "0x...",
      agentName: "Agent",
      nonce: Date.now(),
    };

      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ action, signature, nonce: action.nonce }),
    });

    import { signUserSignedAction } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { ApproveAgentTypes } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import type { AbstractViemLocalAccount } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";

      address: "0x...",
      async signTypedData({ domain, types, primaryType, message }) {
        // Your EIP-712 signing logic (HSM, MPC, remote signer, etc.)
        return "0x...";
      },
    };

      type: "approveAgent",
      signatureChainId: "0x66eee",
      hyperliquidChain: "Mainnet",
      agentAddress: "0x...",
      agentName: "Agent",
      nonce: Date.now(),
    };

    import { createL1ActionHash } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    
    const hash = createL1ActionHash({
      action: { type: "cancel", cancels: [{ a: 0, o: 12345 }] },

Copy

    import { signL1Action, signMultiSigAction } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const signers = [\
      privateKeyToAccount("0x..."), // leader — signs the wrapper\
      privateKeyToAccount("0x..."),\
    ];
    const multiSigUser = "0x..."; // the multi-sig account address
    
    const action = { type: "scheduleCancel", time: Date.now() + 10_000 };
    const nonce = Date.now();
    
    // 1. All signers sign the [user, leader, action] tuple
    const signatures = await Promise.all(signers.map(async (signer) => {
      return await signL1Action({
        wallet: signer,
        action: [multiSigUser.toLowerCase(), signers[0].address.toLowerCase(), action],
        nonce,
        // isTestnet: true,
      });
    }));
    
    // 2. Wrap and sign with leader
    const multiSigAction = {
      type: "multiSig" as const,
      signatureChainId: "0x66eee" as const,
      signatures,
      payload: {
        multiSigUser: multiSigUser.toLowerCase(),
        outerSigner: signers[0].address.toLowerCase(),
        action,
      },
    };
    
    const signature = await signMultiSigAction({
      wallet: signers[0],
      action: multiSigAction,
      nonce,
      // isTestnet: true,
    });
    
    await fetch("https://api.hyperliquid.xyz/exchange", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ action: multiSigAction, signature, nonce }),
    });

Copy

    import { signMultiSigAction, signUserSignedAction } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { UsdSendTypes } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const signers = [\
      privateKeyToAccount("0x..."), // leader — signs the wrapper\
      privateKeyToAccount("0x..."),\
    ];
    const multiSigUser = "0x..."; // the multi-sig account address
    
    const action = {
      type: "usdSend",
      signatureChainId: "0x66eee" as const,
      hyperliquidChain: "Mainnet", // "Testnet" for testnet
      destination: "0x...",
      amount: "100",
      time: Date.now(),
    };
    
    // 1. All signers sign the action with multi-sig fields
    const signatures = await Promise.all(signers.map(async (signer) => {
      return await signUserSignedAction({
        wallet: signer,
        action: {
          payloadMultiSigUser: multiSigUser.toLowerCase() as `0x${string}`,
          outerSigner: signers[0].address.toLowerCase() as `0x${string}`,
          ...action,
        },
        types: UsdSendTypes,
      });
    }));
    
    // 2. Wrap and sign with leader
    const multiSigAction = {
      type: "multiSig",
      signatureChainId: "0x66eee" as const,
      signatures,
      payload: {
        multiSigUser: multiSigUser.toLowerCase(),
        outerSigner: signers[0].address.toLowerCase(),
        action,
      },
    };
    
    const signature = await signMultiSigAction({
      wallet: signers[0],
      action: multiSigAction,
      nonce: action.time,
      // isTestnet: true,
    });
    
    await fetch("https://api.hyperliquid.xyz/exchange", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ action: multiSigAction, signature, nonce: action.time }),
    });

Copy

    import { getWalletAddress, getWalletChainId } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const address = await getWalletAddress(wallet); // "0x..."
    const chainId = await getWalletChainId(wallet); // "0xa4b1"

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Browser wallets | Hyperliquid

The SDK works with browser extension wallets like MetaMask.

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/browser-wallets#setup)

Setup


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

viem

ethers

Connect via a [JSON-RPC Accountarrow-up-right](https://viem.sh/docs/clients/wallet#json-rpc-accounts)
:

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { createWalletClient, custom } from "viem";
    import { arbitrum } from "viem/chains";
    
    const wallet = createWalletClient({
      chain: arbitrum,
      transport: custom(window.ethereum!),
    });
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });

Connect via a [BrowserProviderarrow-up-right](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/providers/#BrowserProvider)
:

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { BrowserProvider } from "ethers";
    
    const provider = new BrowserProvider(window.ethereum!);
    const wallet = await provider.getSigner();
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });

[hashtag](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/browser-wallets#signature-prompts)

Signature prompts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every exchange action triggers a wallet popup that the user must approve. [L1 actions](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#l1-action)
 (trading and position management) show a [phantom agent](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/signing#l1-action)
 hash instead of human-readable details — this is by design, because the action is never signed directly.

To avoid repeated popups and hide unreadable L1 signatures from users, approve an [agent wallet](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults#agent-wallets)
 once with the browser wallet, then use the agent's private key for all subsequent trades:

[PreviousAgent wallets and vaultschevron-left](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/agent-wallets-and-vaults)
[NextTree-shakingchevron-right](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/tree-shaking)

Last updated 5 days ago

*   [Setup](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/browser-wallets#setup)
    
*   [Signature prompts](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/guides/browser-wallets#signature-prompts)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    // 1. Approve agent once (triggers wallet popup)
    await client.approveAgent({
      agentAddress: "0x...",
      agentName: "browser-agent",
    });
    
    // 2. Trade with agent (no popups)
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const agentClient = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."), // agent's private key
    });
    
    await agentClient.order({ orders: [/* ... */], grouping: "na" });

application/json

Request user TWAP slice fills by time.

typeundefined · enumRequired

Type of request.

userstring · min: 42 · max: 42Required

User address.

Pattern: `^0[xX][0-9a-fA-F]+$`

Start time (in ms since epoch).

endTimeany ofOptional

End time (in ms since epoch).

number · nullableOptional

End time (in ms since epoch).

aggregateByTimebooleanOptional

If true, partial fills are aggregated when a crossing order fills multiple resting orders.

200

anyOptional

      user: "0x...",
      startTime: Date.now() - 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24,
    });

# userFills | Hyperliquid

post

https://api.hyperliquid.xyzMainnetchevron-down

https://api.hyperliquid.xyzhttps://api.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz

/infocopy

Request array of user fills.

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

Request array of user fills.

typeundefined · enumRequired

Type of request.

Possible values: `userFills`

userstring · min: 42 · max: 42Required

User address.

Pattern: `^0[xX][0-9a-fA-F]+$`

aggregateByTimebooleanOptional

If true, partial fills are aggregated when a crossing order fills multiple resting orders.

Responses

chevron-right

200

Array of user trade fills.

application/json

Array of user trade fills.

cloidstringOptional

Client Order ID.

Pattern: `^0x[a-fA-F0-9]{32}$`

liquidationobjectOptional

Liquidation details.

Show propertiesplus

coinstringRequired

Asset symbol.

pxstringRequired

Price.

Pattern: `^[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

szstringRequired

Size.

Pattern: `^[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

sidestring · enumRequired

Order side ("B" = Bid/Buy, "A" = Ask/Sell).

Possible values: `B``A`

timenumberRequired

Timestamp when the trade occurred (in ms since epoch).

startPositionstringRequired

Start position size.

Pattern: `^-?[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

dirstringRequired

Direction indicator for frontend display.

closedPnlstringRequired

Realized PnL.

Pattern: `^-?[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

hashstringRequired

L1 transaction hash.

Pattern: `^0x[a-fA-F0-9]{64}$`

oidnumberRequired

Order ID.

crossedbooleanRequired

Indicates if the fill was a taker order.

feestringRequired

Fee charged or rebate received (negative indicates rebate).

Pattern: `^-?[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

builderFeestringOptional

Optional fee charged by the UI builder.

Pattern: `^-?[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

tidnumberRequired

Unique transaction identifier for a partial fill of an order.

feeTokenstringRequired

Token in which the fee is denominated (e.g., "USDC").

twapIdnumber · nullableRequired

ID of the TWAP.

chevron-right

422

Failed to deserialize the JSON body into the target type

text/plain

chevron-right

500

Internal Server Error

application/json

post

/info

TypeScript

Test it

200

Array of user trade fills.

*   `"activated"`: Active and executing.
*   `"terminated"`: Terminated.
*   `"error"`: An error occurred.

# webData2 | Hyperliquid

post

https://api.hyperliquid.xyzMainnetchevron-down

https://api.hyperliquid.xyzhttps://api.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz

/infocopy

Request comprehensive user and market data.

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

Request comprehensive user and market data.

typeundefined · enumRequired

Type of request.

Possible values: `webData2`

userstring · min: 42 · max: 42Required

User address.

Pattern: `^0[xX][0-9a-fA-F]+$`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Comprehensive user and market data.

application/json

Comprehensive user and market data.

totalVaultEquitystringRequired

Total equity in vaults.

Pattern: `^[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

agentAddressstring · nullableRequired

Agent address if one exists.

Pattern: `^0x[a-fA-F0-9]{40}$`

agentValidUntilnumber · nullableRequired

Timestamp until which the agent is valid.

cumLedgerstringRequired

Cumulative ledger value.

Pattern: `^[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+)?$`

assetCtxsPerpAssetCtxSchema\[\]Required

Array of contexts for each perpetual asset.

serverTimenumberRequired

Server timestamp (in ms since epoch).

isVaultbooleanRequired

Whether this account is a vault.

userstringRequired

User address.

Pattern: `^0x[a-fA-F0-9]{40}$`

twapStatesany\[\]\[\]Required

Array of tuples containing TWAP order ID and its state.

Show propertiesplus

spotAssetCtxsSpotAssetCtxSchema\[\]Required

Asset context for each spot asset.

optOutOfSpotDustingboolean · enumOptional

Whether the user has opted out of spot dusting.

Possible values: `true`
